    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
     // Search keyword mappings
const searchMappings = {
    'rings': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/rings/index.html',
    'necklaces': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/neckpieces/index.html',
    'bracelets': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/bracelet-project/index.html',
    'earrings': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/earrings/index.html',
    'Hair Accessories':'http://127.0.0.1:5500/hair%20accesories/index.html',
    'Luxe':'http://127.0.0.1:5500/lucx/index.html',
    'Party Night Collection': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/party-night-proj/index.html',
    'Diamond Collection': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/diamond%20collection/index.html',
    'Wedding Collection': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/wedding/index.html',
    'Desi Collection': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/desi-collection/index.html',
    'All Jewel': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/alljewels-project/index.html',
    'Anklets': 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/Anklets/index.html'
};

// Populate suggestions
const suggestions = Object.keys(searchMappings);
const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input');
const suggestionsList = document.getElementById('suggestions');

// Autocomplete and suggestions
searchInput.addEventListener('input', function () {
    const query = searchInput.value.toLowerCase().trim();
    suggestionsList.innerHTML = '';

    if (query) {
        const filteredSuggestions = suggestions.filter(item => item.includes(query));
        filteredSuggestions.forEach(item => {
            const highlighted = item.replace(new RegExp(query, 'gi'), match => `<span class="highlight">${match}</span>`);
            const li = document.createElement('li');
            li.innerHTML = highlighted;
            li.setAttribute('data-value', item); // Store the original value
            li.addEventListener('click', () => {
                searchInput.value = item; // Update search input
                suggestionsList.innerHTML = ''; // Clear suggestions
                searchInput.focus(); // Focus back on input for further edits
            });
            suggestionsList.appendChild(li);
        });
    }
});

// Redirect on search button click
document.querySelector('.search-button').addEventListener('click', function () {
    const query = searchInput.value.toLowerCase().trim();

    if (searchMappings[query]) {
        window.location.href = searchMappings[query]; // Redirect to mapped page
    } else {
        window.location.href = 'search-results.html'; // Redirect to a default search results page
    }
});

// Close button functionality
document.querySelector('.close-button').addEventListener('click', function () {
    window.location.href = 'index.html'; // Replace with your home page URL
});

// Clear suggestions on blur
searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
    setTimeout(() => (suggestionsList.innerHTML = ''), 100); // Delay to allow click event to register
});


    </script>
</body>
</html>

    function redirectToHome() {
      var email = document.getElementById('email').value;
      var password = document.getElementById('password').value;

      if (email === "" || password === "") {
        alert("Please fill in both the email and password fields.");
      } else {
        window.location.href = 'http://127.0.0.1:5500/x/index.html'; // Replace with your desired URL
      }
    }

  <script>
    // Function to add an item to the wishlist
    function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
      let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
      wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
      localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
      alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      updateWishlistView(); // Immediately update the view
    }

    // Function to dynamically update the wishlist view
    function updateWishlistView() {
      const cartItems = document.getElementById('cart-items');
      const wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];

      cartItems.innerHTML = ""; // Clear the list
      const contentHeading = document.querySelector('.content h2');
      const contentParagraph = document.querySelector('.content p');

      if (wishlist.length > 0) {
        contentHeading.textContent = "Your Wishlist";
        contentParagraph.textContent = "Here are the items you wish for:";
        wishlist.forEach((item, index) => {
          const listItem = document.createElement('li');
          listItem.innerHTML = `
            <img src="${item.image}" alt="${item.name}">
            <span>${item.name}</span>
            <span>‚Çπ${item.price}</span>
            <button " class="buy-now-btn" onclick="redirectToPayment('${item.name}', ${item.price})">BuyNow</button>
            <button class="remove-btn" onclick="removeFromWishlist(${index})">Remove</button>`;
          cartItems.appendChild(listItem);
        });
      } else {
        contentHeading.textContent = "Your wishlist is empty.";
        contentParagraph.textContent = "Let‚Äôs fill it up with some amazing jewellery!";
      }
    }

    // Function to redirect to payment page
    function redirectToPayment(productName, price) {
      // Save the selected product details to localStorage
      localStorage.setItem('selectedProduct', JSON.stringify({ name: productName, price: price }));
      // Redirect to the payment page
      window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    }

    // Function to remove an item from the wishlist
    function removeFromWishlist(index) {
      let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
      wishlist.splice(index, 1); // Remove the item at the given index
      localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
      updateWishlistView(); // Reload the wishlist dynamically
    }

    // Load wishlist items when the page is loaded
    window.onload = updateWishlistView;
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  <!-- JavaScript for cart functionality -->
  <script>
    window.onload = function () {
      // Get the cart from localStorage
      let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];

      // Get the cart items list element
      const cartItemsList = document.getElementById("cart-items");

      // Get the empty cart message elements
      const emptyMessage = document.querySelector(".content h2");
      const emptySubMessage = document.querySelector(".content p");

      // Function to render the cart items
      function renderCart() {
        cartItemsList.innerHTML = ""; // Clear the cart items list

        if (cart.length === 0) {
          // Show the empty cart message
          emptyMessage.style.display = "block";
          emptySubMessage.style.display = "block";
        } else {
          // Hide the empty cart message
          emptyMessage.style.display = "none";
          emptySubMessage.style.display = "none";

          // Populate the cart items dynamically
          cart.forEach((item, index) => {
            const li = document.createElement("li");

            // Create an image element for the product
            const img = document.createElement("img");
            img.src = item.image;
            img.alt = item.name;
            img.width = 50;
            img.style.marginRight = "10px";

            // Create text for the item (name and price)
            const itemText = document.createTextNode(`${item.name} - $${item.price}`);

            // Create a Remove button
            const removeBtn = document.createElement("button");
            removeBtn.textContent = "Remove";
            removeBtn.style.marginLeft = "10px";
            removeBtn.style.backgroundColor = "#FF4D4D";
            removeBtn.style.color = "white";
            removeBtn.style.border = "none";
            removeBtn.style.padding = "5px 10px";
            removeBtn.style.borderRadius = "5px";
            removeBtn.style.cursor = "pointer";

            // Add event listener to the Remove button
            removeBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
              cart.splice(index, 1); // Remove the item from the cart array
              localStorage.setItem("cart", JSON.stringify(cart)); // Update localStorage
              renderCart(); // Re-render the cart
            });

            // Create a Buy Now button
            const buyNowBtn = document.createElement("button");
            buyNowBtn.textContent = "Buy Now";
            buyNowBtn.style.marginLeft = "10px";
            buyNowBtn.style.backgroundColor = "#4CAF50";
            buyNowBtn.style.color = "white";
            buyNowBtn.style.border = "none";
            buyNowBtn.style.padding = "5px 10px";
            buyNowBtn.style.borderRadius = "5px";
            buyNowBtn.style.cursor = "pointer";

            // Add event listener to the Buy Now button
            buyNowBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  // Redirect to the payment page
  window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html"; // Replace with the actual path to your payment page
});

            // Append elements to the list item
            li.appendChild(img);
            li.appendChild(itemText);
            li.appendChild(removeBtn); // Add Remove button
            li.appendChild(buyNowBtn); // Add Buy Now button

            // Add the list item to the cart list
            cartItemsList.appendChild(li);
          });
        }
      }

      // Initial render
      renderCart();
    };
  </script>
</body>
</html>

            border: 2px solid #333;

        #camera {

        /* Jewelry overlay styling */
        .jewelry {
            position: absolute;
            width: 100px; /* adjust as needed */
            transition: transform 0.1s ease;
        }
        .controls {
            margin-top: 10px;

<body>

    <h1>Virtual Jewelry Try-On</h1>
    <div class="camera-container">
        <video id="camera" autoplay></video>
        <canvas id="overlay"></canvas>
    </div>

    <div class="controls">
        <button onclick="startCamera()">Start Camera</button>
        <label for="jewelrySelect">Choose Jewelry:</label>
        <select id="jewelrySelect" onchange="changeJewelry(this.value)">
            <option value="necklace">Necklace</option>
            <option value="earrings">Earrings</option>
            <option value="bracelet">Bracelet</option>
        </select>
    </div>

    <script>
        let video = document.getElementById('camera');
        let overlayCanvas = document.getElementById('overlay');
        let context = overlayCanvas.getContext('2d');

        // Start webcam
        async function startCamera() {
            try {
                const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: true });
                video.srcObject = stream;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
            }
        }

        // Set default jewelry image
        let jewelryImg = new Image();
        jewelryImg.src = 'https://blingbag.co.in/cdn/shop/files/EmeraldTeresaZirconiaJewellerySet_4_1800x1800-Photoroom_1080x.jpg?v=1723277682'; // default jewelry

        // Draw jewelry overlay
        function drawJewelry() {
            context.clearRect(0, 0, overlayCanvas.width, overlayCanvas.height);
            overlayCanvas.width = video.videoWidth;
            overlayCanvas.height = video.videoHeight;

            // Position jewelry based on face detection or set default position
            let x = video.videoWidth / 2 - 50; // adjust position
            let y = video.videoHeight / 2; // adjust position
            context.drawImage(jewelryImg, x, y, 100, 100); // adjust size
            requestAnimationFrame(drawJewelry);
        }

        // Change jewelry
        function changeJewelry(type) {
            if (type === 'necklace') {
                jewelryImg.src = 'path_to_images/necklace.png';
            } else if (type === 'earrings') {
                jewelryImg.src = 'path_to_images/earrings.png';
            } else if (type === 'bracelet') {
                jewelryImg.src = 'path_to_images/bracelet.png';
            }
            jewelryImg.onload = () => requestAnimationFrame(drawJewelry); // Start drawing when the image is loaded
        }

        // Start drawing when the video is playing
        video.addEventListener('play', () => {
            overlayCanvas.width = video.videoWidth; // set width to match video
            overlayCanvas.height = video.videoHeight; // set height to match video
            requestAnimationFrame(drawJewelry);
        });
    </script>

</body>
</html>

    <script>
           document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>

document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
});

      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {

      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
       document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
      document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

    <script>
         document.querySelectorAll('.Buynow').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const price = this.getAttribute('data-price');
        const paymentUrl = `https://www.example.com/payment?amount=${price}`;
        window.location.href = "http://127.0.0.1:5500/payment-project/index.html";
    });
})
      // Add to Cart functionality
      function addToCart(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        cart.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your cart!`);
      }

      // Add to Wishlist functionality
      function addToWishlist(productName, price, imageSrc) {
        let wishlist = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('wishlist')) || [];
        wishlist.push({ name: productName, price: price, image: imageSrc });
        localStorage.setItem('wishlist', JSON.stringify(wishlist));
        alert(`${productName} has been added to your wishlist!`);
      }
    </script>

            <h2>Shipping</h2>
            <h3>COD & Online Pre-Paid</h3>
            <p>We offer shipping for all orders across India. Currently, we do not provide international shipping.</p>
            <h3>Online Pre-Paid Orders</h3>
            <p>All orders below INR 200 must be prepaid, including a shipping charge of INR 60.</p>
            <h3>Pay on Delivery/Cash on Delivery/Online Prepaid Orders</h3>
            <p>Orders exceeding INR 200 can be placed as COD/POD or Online Prepaid orders. A shipping fee of INR 60 is applicable to orders below INR 600. Free shipping is provided for orders valued above INR 600. COD is available for a maximum order value of up to INR 4999. For orders exceeding INR 5000, only prepaid orders are accepted. We accept payments via Net Banking, Debit Card, Credit Card, UPI, Paytm, Cash on Delivery, and Pay on Delivery. All prices include GST.</p>

    <section id="delivery">
        <div class="container">
            <h2>Delivery</h2>
            <h3>Express Delivery</h3>
            <p>Standard shipping for Express Delivery Tag Products is within 5-7 business days, with variations based on the shipping address and pin code. You will receive a notification on your registered contact number and email once the order is shipped. Exchange services are not available; we exclusively offer Replacement or Store Credit options for COD and POD orders.</p>
            <h3>Standard Delivery</h3>
            <p>Our courier partners deliver from Monday to Saturday, excluding public holidays, with a delivery window from 10:00 AM to 6:00 PM. Shipping durations differ based on the product, as indicated on respective product pages. Standard shipping typically takes 3-7 business days, while make-to-order items may require an additional 5-7 days. If an order includes multiple products, the longest shipping time applies.</p>
            <h3>Delivery Procedure & Notifications</h3>
            <p>A notification will be sent to the registered contact number and email address upon the order being shipped from our warehouse. Address changes are permitted if the order has not been shipped. Once the status is "Ready to Ship" with an AWB No, it will be processed at the provided address. It is mandatory to include an email address in each order for effective communication. Upon shipping, the customer will receive an SMS on their registered number and an email containing the order and tracking details. The company is not responsible for delays caused by natural disasters or unforeseeable events. We will aid in tracking parcels in case of issues arising from the delivery partner's side. Refrain from disclosing any OTP to the delivery partner until your order has been successfully delivered to you at your given shipping address. NOTE: If a customer rejects three separate COD/POD orders, the system will automatically designate them for prepaid orders exclusively in the future. For any further information on delivery or shipping details contact us at: Email ID: care@everstylish.com Contact Us: +91 8882188858 Business Hours: Monday - Saturday 10:00AM ‚Äì 6:00PM (IST)</p>
        </div>

            <h2>Return & Refunds</h2>
            <p>The timeline to raise a return request is within 72 hours from the date of order delivery. Kindly ensure that you have an unboxing video of the delivered package to facilitate a seamless return process.</p>
            <h3>For Pay on Delivery/Cash on Delivery Orders</h3>
            <p>Store credits or replacement for the same product will be provided, depending on the selected return resolution. Refunds cannot be transferred to any other payment method. Once we receive your return order, we will send you an email to confirm the receipt of the parcel and proceed with your selected mode of resolution method.</p>
            <h3>For Online Pre-Paid Orders (Net Banking/Debit Card/Credit Card/UPI/Other Wallets)</h3>
            <p>We will reimburse the original source account within 7-10 business days upon receiving the items with original labels and tags, excluding the delivery fee. For orders paid with a card, the refund will be credited to the same card used during the order placement. For orders paid through UPI, the refund will be transferred to the same UPI ID.</p>

    <section id="order-faqs">
        <div class="container">
            <h2>Order</h2>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.1 How will I know if the order is successfully placed?</h3>
                <p>Ans. An SMS and email confirmation containing order details will be sent to your registered email address and contact number.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.2 How can I check the status of my order?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Sign into your registered account on our website or app. Go to ‚ÄúMy Account‚Äù ‚Üí ‚ÄúMy Orders‚Äù to check your order history or status.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.3 How can I track my order?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Upon shipment of the order, a Tracking ID will be mailed to you along with the link. Alternatively, you can sign in, and navigate to "My Account" ‚Üí "My Orders" ‚Üí "Track Order" to access all the updates on your shipment.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.4 What is the estimated delivery time?</h3>
                <p>Ans. The shipping timeline differs by product, as mentioned on the respective product page. Standard shipping takes up to 3-7 business days from the date of shipping. Make-to-order items take an additional 5-7 business days. When multiple products are included in a single order, the longest shipping timeline is applicable.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.5 Can I get my order delivered earlier or on a specific date?</h3>
                <p>Ans. For expedited delivery requests, log in and submit a ticket through the Help Desk in "My Account" or email us at care@everstylish.com. You can also contact Customer Care at 8882188858 for prompt assistance with your order.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.6 Can I get my orders delivered at a specific time?</h3>
                <p>Ans. You have the option to synchronize your availability with the delivery person, who will connect with you at the time of order delivery. If any issues arise, feel free to reach us via email at care@everstylish.com or contact our Customer Care at 8882188858.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.7 Do you have OTP Verification at the time of order delivery?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Certainly, an OTP will be sent through SMS to your registered contact number for cancellation or delivery. It is recommended not to share the OTP unless the courier partner is at your doorstep with your order. If there are any suspicions or inappropriate behaviour, please report it to us at care@everstylish.com.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.8 How do I cancel my order?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Initiate a cancellation, log in to your registered account and navigate to ‚ÄúMy Account‚Äù ‚Üí ‚ÄúMy Orders‚Äù ‚Üí ‚ÄúRequest Cancellation.‚Äù If the order has not been shipped, it will be cancelled automatically.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.9 Can I change the shipping address of my order after it has been placed?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Certainly, you can update the shipping address of your order prior to it being processed for shipping. For assistance, you can use the Helpdesk in My Account, contact us via email at care@everstylish.com or call us at 8882188858.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.10 Can I change the shipping address of my order after it has been shipped or when the order is in transit?</h3>
                <p>Ans. The shipping address cannot be altered once the order is dispatched. However, you can add an alternate contact number or additional information to the existing shipping address on your order.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.11 Do you have Free Shipping?</h3>
                <p>Ans. FREE shipping is provided for all orders exceeding INR 600/-. The orders below this value are subject to a shipping fee of Rs.60/-.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.12 What to do if my order has an item missing or damaged?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Please provide an unboxing video of your order and reach out to us at care@everstylish.com or +91 8882188858.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.13 How can I get information regarding the delay in delivery?</h3>
                <p>Ans. If there is a delay in the shipment, please email us at care@everstylish.com or reach us at +91 8882188858.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq">
                <h3>Q.14 What if the order is not delivered?</h3>
                <p>Ans. Listed below are potential resolutions for orders undelivered to customers or those marked as Return to Origin (RTO).</p>
                <ul>
                    <li>(a) For Cash on Delivery/Pay on Delivery orders, if the courier person fails to deliver after three attempts, the order will be sent back to our warehouse. You can now proceed to place a new order with us.</li>
                    <li>(b) For prepaid orders, upon receiving the order at our warehouse, we will contact you. You can either choose to have the order re-shipped to the specified shipping address or opt for a refund.</li>
                </ul>
            </div>
        </div>
